\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The \doxylink{classbt_soft_body}{bt\+Soft\+Body} is an class to simulate cloth and volumetric soft bodies. There is two-\/way interaction between \doxylink{classbt_soft_body}{bt\+Soft\+Body} and bt\+Rigid\+Body/bt\+Collision\+Object.
